"!######################################################################################
 
SYSTEM 1 - Series setup (FC => VCC, ST parallel)
 
Author: Rasmus Øxenhave
Date: may 2016
Version: 3
 
#######################################################################################"
 
$UNITSYSTEM SI K bar kJ
"define units"
$arrays on "off -> show only in solution window"
$SumRow off "Sum rows in parametric table"
$Bookmark test
$TabStops 0.5 1 1.5 2 2.5 cm
 
$CheckUnits Off
$CheckUnits On
//X = Lookup('Lookup 1', Lookuprow('Lookup 1','UAaa',UA), 'Tamb_lim')
 
procedure P001( hour, input_T1, input_T3, input_Tamb, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100, Q_dot_d, Q_storage_i0,V_ST,
V_ST_C_i0,W_dot_fan_nom,m_dot_fan_nom, DELTAT_pinch_C,DELTAT_pinch_E,DELTAT_EtoCmin, eta_Ct : 
FCmode$, T11_limit,Q_dot_FC,Q_dot_VCC,Q_dot_st_charge, Q_dot_st_discharge, m_dot_a,m_dot_w,
m_dot_ST_charge_max, m_dot_ST_discharge_max, m_dot_ST_charge, m_dot_ST_discharge, V_st_C,Q_st, T2, T12, 
W_dot_FC, W_dot_VCC,UA,cap_speed )
"========================================================="
"Demand"
T1 = converttemp(C,K,input_T1)
T3 = converttemp(C,K,input_T3)
h1 = enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T1)
h3 = enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T3)
rho3 = Density(Water,P=p_w,T=T3)
m_dot_w_d = Q_dot_d / (h1-h3) 
V_dot_w_d = m_dot_w_d * 3600 [s/h] / rho3
 
"Ambient"
Tamb = converttemp(C,K,input_Tamb)
T11 = IF(Tamb, T1, Tamb, T1-0.01[K], Tamb)
 
"Fans: Amount, Power and MassFlow"
N_fan = UA_100 / (160 [kW/K]) *16
"Number of fans at freecooler"
W_dot_fan_nom1 = N_fan*W_dot_fan_nom "Nominal fan power (combined)"
m_dot_fan_nom1 = N_fan*m_dot_fan_nom "Nominal fan mass flow (combined)"
 
"========================================================="
"Storage limitations and size"
V_ST_C_max = V_ST
V_ST_C_min = 0 [m^3]
 
m_ST_C_max = V_ST_C_max * rho3
m_ST_C_i0 = V_ST_C_i0 * rho3
 
m_dot_ST_discharge_max = max( m_ST_C_i0/3600 [s] , 0 [kg/s])
m_dot_ST_charge_max =max( (m_ST_C_max - m_ST_C_i0)/3600 [s] , 0 [kg/s])
"========================================================="
 
call Limit(m_dot_fan_nom1,T1, T3, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100 : T11_limit )
 
"!----------------------------------------------------"
"!new"
 
x = 8760[h] - (V_st_C_max/V_dot_w_d)
y = 8760[h] - (V_st_C_i0/V_dot_w_d)
 
IF (hour >= x) AND (hour>=y) AND (m_dot_ST_discharge_max > m_dot_w_d) THEN
 
FCmode$ = 'State 4' 
m_dot_a = 0 [kg/s]
m_dot_w = m_dot_w_d
m_dot_ST_charge = 0 [kg/s] 
160
APPENDIX H. EES MODEL - SYSTEM 1
==PAGE:175==

6/24/2016 4:28:06 AM  Page 2
EES Ver. 10.055: #0780: Department of Energy Engineering, Tech. Univ. of Denmark
m_dot_ST_discharge = m_dot_w_d
Q_dot_FC = 0 [kW]
Q_dot_VCC = 0 [kW]
Q_dot_st_charge = 0 [kW]
Q_dot_st_discharge = m_dot_ST_discharge * (h1-h3)
T2 = 0 [K] 
T12 = 0 [K]
UA = 0 [kW/K]
cap_speed = 0 [-]
 
ELSE
"!new end"
 
IF ( Tamb < T11_limit ) THEN
FCmode$ = 'State 1a'
call FCmaxAirST(T1, T3, T11, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100, m_dot_fan_nom1 : Q_dot_FC, 
m_dot_a,m_dot_w, UA,cap_speed, T2, T12 )
 
IF ( m_dot_w - m_dot_w_d > m_dot_ST_charge_max ) THEN 
FCmode$ = 'State 1b' 
Call FCvarAirST(T1, T3, T11, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0,UA_100, m_dot_fan_nom1,
m_dot_ST_charge_max : Q_dot_FC, m_dot_a,m_dot_w, UA,cap_speed, T2, T12 )
ENDIF
m_dot_ST_charge = m_dot_w - m_dot_w_d
m_dot_ST_discharge = 0 [kg/s]
Q_dot_st_charge = Q_dot_FC - Q_dot_d
Q_dot_st_discharge = 0 [kW]
Q_dot_FC = Q_dot_FC
Q_dot_VCC = max( Q_dot_d - Q_dot_FC, 0[kW])
ELSE
IF ( Tamb < T3 ) THEN
FCmode$ = 'State 3'
Call FCmaxAirT2(T1, T3, T11, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100, m_dot_fan_nom1 : Q_dot_FC, 
m_dot_a,m_dot_w, UA,cap_speed, T2, T12 )
m_dot_st_discharge_need = m_dot_w_d - m_dot_w
IF ( m_dot_st_discharge_need > m_dot_ST_discharge_max ) THEN
FCmode$ = 'State 6a'
call FCmaxAir(T1, T3, T11, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100, m_dot_fan_nom1 : Q_dot_FC, 
m_dot_a,m_dot_w, UA,cap_speed, T2, T12 )
ENDIF
 
m_dot_ST_charge = 0 [kg/s]
m_dot_ST_discharge = m_dot_w_d - m_dot_w
Q_dot_st_charge = 0 [kW]
Q_dot_st_discharge = m_dot_ST_discharge * (h1-h3)
 
Q_dot_FC = Q_dot_FC
Q_dot_VCC = if( Q_dot_st_discharge, 0, Q_dot_d - Q_dot_FC, Q_dot_d - Q_dot_FC, 0 [kW])
ELSE
IF ( Tamb < T1 ) THEN
IF ( m_dot_ST_discharge_max > m_dot_w_d ) THEN
FCmode$ = 'State 4'
Q_dot_FC = 0 [kW]
m_dot_a = 0 [kg/s];
m_dot_w = 0 [kg/s]
UA = UA_0
;
cap_speed = 0
T2 = 273.15 [K]
;
T12 =273.15 [K]
ELSE
FCmode$ = 'State 6b'
call FCmaxAir(T1, T3, T11, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100, m_dot_fan_nom1 : Q_dot_FC,
 m_dot_a,m_dot_w, UA,cap_speed, T2, T12 )
ENDIF
m_dot_ST_charge = 0 [kg/s]
m_dot_ST_discharge = m_dot_w_d - m_dot_w

Q_dot_st_charge = 0 [kW]
Q_dot_st_discharge = m_dot_ST_discharge * (h1-h3)
 
Q_dot_FC = Q_dot_FC
Q_dot_VCC = if( Q_dot_st_discharge, Q_dot_d, Q_dot_d - Q_dot_FC, 0[kW], 0 [kW])
 
ELSE "Tamb > T1"
 
IF ( m_dot_ST_discharge_max > m_dot_w_d ) THEN
FCmode$ = 'State 4'
m_dot_ST_discharge = m_dot_w_d
ELSE
IF ( m_dot_ST_discharge_max > 0 [kg/s] ) THEN
FCmode$ = 'State 7'
m_dot_ST_discharge = m_dot_ST_discharge_max
ELSE
FCmode$ = 'State 8'
m_dot_ST_discharge = 0 [kg/s]
ENDIF
ENDIF
 
m_dot_w = m_dot_w_d - m_dot_ST_discharge
m_dot_a = 0 [kg/s]
UA = UA_0
cap_speed = 0
T2 = T1
T12 =Tamb
 
m_dot_ST_charge = 0 [kg/s]
Q_dot_st_charge = 0 [kW]
Q_dot_st_discharge = m_dot_ST_discharge * (h1-h3)
Q_dot_FC = 0 [kW]
Q_dot_VCC = max( Q_dot_d - Q_dot_st_discharge, 0[kW])
 
ENDIF
ENDIF
ENDIF 
ENDIF 
 
 
"!Storage"
Q_st = Q_storage_i0 + m_dot_st_charge*h3*3600[s]*convert('kJ','MWh') - m_dot_st_discharge*h3*3600[s]*convert('kJ','
MWh')
m_ST_C = m_ST_C_i0 + m_dot_ST_charge*3600[s] - m_dot_ST_discharge*3600[s] 
 
V_ST_C = m_ST_C / rho3
 
 
"!Work / power consumption and COP"
T_E = T3 - DELTAT_pinch_E
T_C = IF( Tamb+DELTAT_pinch_C,T_E+DELTAT_EtoCmin,T_E+DELTAT_EtoCmin,T_E+DELTAT_EtoCmin,Tamb+
DELTAT_pinch_C)
Q_dot_E = Q_dot_VCC
"Ref cycle heat transfer"
COP_carnot = (T_E)/( T_C - T_E )
"COP carnot = TC / (TH - TC)"
COP_VCC = COP_carnot * eta_Ct
"Ref cycle COP"
 
W_dot_VCC = Q_dot_E / COP_VCC
"Ref cycle power consumption"
 
IF(Q_dot_FC > 0) THEN
W_dot_FC = W_dot_fan_nom1 * cap_speed^2.8
ELSE
W_dot_FC = 0
ENDIF
 
IF (Q_dot_VCC = 0) THEN
COP_VCC = 0
ELSE
COP_VCC = COP_VCC

EES Ver. 10.055: #0780: Department of Energy Engineering, Tech. Univ. of Denmark
ENDIF
 
IF (W_dot_FC = 0) THEN
COP_FC = 0
ELSE
COP_FC = Q_dot_FC / W_dot_FC
ENDIF
 
 
end
 
 
"#####################################################################"
 
subprogram Limit(m_dot_fan_nom1,T1, T3, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a,UA_0, UA_100 : T11 )
"! Limit
Calculate at which ambient temperature the FC at max air flow can supply demand (mass flow water = m_dot_w_d)"
"Assumptions"
m_dot_a = m_dot_fan_nom1
T2 = T3
Q_dot_d = Q_dot_FC
 
"Calculations"
cap_speed = ((UA - UA_0)/(UA_100 - UA_0))^(1/0.8)
cap_speed = m_dot_a / m_dot_fan_nom1 
 
h1=enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T1)
h2=enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T2)
h11=enthalpy(air_HA,p=p_a,T=T11)
h12=enthalpy(air_HA,p=p_a,T=T12)
 
Q_dot_FC = UA*LMTD
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_w*(h1-h2)
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_a*(h12-h11)
 
 
DELTAT1 = T1-T12
DELTAT2 = T2-T11
DELTAT_pinch = min(DELTAT1, DELTAT2)
"pinch temperature"
LMTD = ( (DELTAT1^0.3275 + DELTAT2^0.3275) / 2 )^(1/0.3275)
 
end
 
"#####################################################################"
 
subprogram FCmaxAirST(T1, T3, T11, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100, m_dot_fan_nom1 : Q_dot_FC,

h11=enthalpy(air_HA,p=p_a,T=T11)
h12=enthalpy(air_HA,p=p_a,T=T12)
 
Q_dot_FC = UA*LMTD
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_w*(h1-h2)
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_a*(h12-h11)
 
DELTAT1 = T1-T12
DELTAT2 = T2-T11

subprogram FCmaxAirT2(T1, T3, T11, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100, m_dot_fan_nom1 : Q_dot_FC,

"!######################################################################################
 
SYSTEM 2 - Series setup (VCC => FC, ST parallel)
 
Author: Rasmus Øxenhave
Date: march 2016
Version: 2
 
#######################################################################################"
 
$UNITSYSTEM SI K bar kJ
"define units"
$arrays on "off -> show only in solution window"
$SumRow off "Sum rows in parametric table"
$Bookmark test
$TabStops 0.5 1 1.5 2 2.5 cm
 
$CheckUnits Off
$CheckUnits On
//X = Lookup('Lookup 1', Lookuprow('Lookup 1','UAaa',UA), 'Tamb_lim')
 
procedure P001(hour,  input_T1, input_T3, input_Tamb, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100, Q_dot_d, Q_storage_i0,V_ST,
V_ST_C_i0,W_dot_fan_nom,m_dot_fan_nom, DELTAT_pinch_C,DELTAT_pinch_E,DELTAT_EtoCmin, eta_Ct : 
FCmode$, T11_limit,Q_dot_FC,Q_dot_VCC,Q_dot_st_charge, Q_dot_st_discharge, m_dot_a,m_dot_w,
m_dot_ST_charge_max, m_dot_ST_discharge_max, m_dot_ST_charge, m_dot_ST_discharge, V_st_C,Q_st, T2, T12, 
W_dot_FC, W_dot_VCC,UA,cap_speed )
"========================================================="
"Demand"
T1 = converttemp(C,K,input_T1)
T3 = converttemp(C,K,input_T3)
h1 = enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T1)
h3 = enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T3)
rho3 = Density(Water,P=p_w,T=T3)
m_dot_w_d = Q_dot_d / (h1-h3) 
V_dot_w_d = m_dot_w_d * 3600 [s/h] / rho3
 
"Ambient"
Tamb = converttemp(C,K,input_Tamb)
T11 = IF(Tamb, T1, Tamb, T1-0.01[K], Tamb)
 
"Fans: Amount, Power and MassFlow"
N_fan = UA_100 / (160 [kW/K]) *16
"Number of fans at freecooler"
W_dot_fan_nom1 = N_fan*W_dot_fan_nom "Nominal fan power (combined)"
m_dot_fan_nom1 = N_fan*m_dot_fan_nom "Nominal fan mass flow (combined)"
 
"========================================================="
"Storage limitations and size"
V_ST_C_max = V_ST
V_ST_C_min = 0 [m^3]
 
m_ST_C_max = V_ST_C_max * rho3
m_ST_C_i0 = V_ST_C_i0 * rho3
 
m_dot_ST_discharge_max = m_ST_C_i0/3600 [s]
m_dot_ST_charge_max = (m_ST_C_max - m_ST_C_i0)/3600 [s]
"========================================================="
 
call Limit(m_dot_fan_nom1,T1, T3, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100 : T11_limit )
 
"!new"
x = 8760[h] - (V_st_C_max/V_dot_w_d)
y = 8760[h] - (V_st_C_i0/V_dot_w_d)
 
IF (hour >= x) AND (hour>=y) AND (m_dot_ST_discharge_max > m_dot_w_d) THEN
 
FCmode$ = 'State 4' 
m_dot_a = 0 [kg/s]
m_dot_w = m_dot_w_d
m_dot_ST_charge = 0 [kg/s] 
m_dot_ST_discharge = m_dot_w_d
Q_dot_FC = 0 [kW]

IF ( m_dot_ST_discharge_max > m_dot_w_d ) THEN
FCmode$ = 'State 4'
m_dot_ST_discharge = m_dot_w_d

m_dot_ST_discharge = m_dot_ST_discharge_max

m_dot_w = m_dot_w_d - m_dot_ST_discharge
m_dot_a = 0 [kg/s]
UA = UA_0
cap_speed = 0

subprogram Limit(m_dot_fan_nom1,T1, T3, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a,UA_0, UA_100 : T11 )
"! Limit
Calculate at which ambient temperature the FC at max air flow can supply demand (mass flow water = m_dot_w_d)"
"Assumptions"
m_dot_a = m_dot_fan_nom1
T2 = T1
Q_dot_d = Q_dot_FC

"!######################################################################################
 
SYSTEM 3 - Parallel setup (ST, FC, VCC) 
 
Author: Rasmus Øxenhave
Date: march 2016
Version: 1
 
#######################################################################################"
 
$UNITSYSTEM SI K bar kJ
"define units"
$arrays on "off -> show only in solution window"
$SumRow off "Sum rows in parametric table"
$Bookmark test
$TabStops 0.5 1 1.5 2 2.5 cm
 
$CheckUnits Off
$CheckUnits On
 
 
procedure P001(hour,  input_T1, input_T3, input_Tamb, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100, Q_dot_d, Q_storage_i0,V_ST,
V_ST_C_i0,W_dot_fan_nom,m_dot_fan_nom, DELTAT_pinch_C,DELTAT_pinch_E,DELTAT_EtoCmin, DELTAT_offset,
eta_Ct : FCmode$, T11_limit,Q_dot_FC,Q_dot_VCC,Q_dot_st_charge, Q_dot_st_discharge, m_dot_a,m_dot_w_d,
m_dot_w,m_dot_w_FC,m_dot_w_VCC,m_dot_ST_charge_max, m_dot_ST_discharge_max, m_dot_ST_charge, 
m_dot_ST_discharge, V_st_C,Q_st, T3_FC,T3_VCC, T12, W_dot_FC, W_dot_VCC,UA )
 
"========================================================="
"Demand"
T1 = converttemp(C,K,input_T1)
T3 = converttemp(C,K,input_T3)
h1 = enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T1)
h3 = enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T3)
rho3 = Density(Water,P=p_w,T=T3)
m_dot_w_d = Q_dot_d / (h1-h3) 
V_dot_w_d = m_dot_w_d * 3600 [s/h] / rho3
 
"Ambient"
Tamb = converttemp(C,K,input_Tamb)
T11 = IF(Tamb, T1, Tamb, T1-0.01[K], Tamb)
 
"Fans: Amount, Power and MassFlow"
N_fan = UA_100 / (160 [kW/K]) *16
"Number of fans at freecooler"
W_dot_fan_nom1 = N_fan*W_dot_fan_nom "Total nominal fan power"
m_dot_fan_nom1 = N_fan*m_dot_fan_nom "Total nominal air mass flow rate"
 
"Storage limitations and size"
V_ST_C_max = V_ST
V_ST_C_min = 0 [m^3]
 
m_ST_C_max = V_ST_C_max * rho3
m_ST_C_i0 = V_ST_C_i0 * rho3
 
m_dot_ST_discharge_max = m_ST_C_i0/3600 [s]
m_dot_ST_charge_max = (m_ST_C_max - m_ST_C_i0)/3600 [s]
"========================================================="
 
call Limit(m_dot_fan_nom1,T1, T3, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100 : T11_limit )
 
 
"!new"
x = 8760[h] - (V_st_C_max/V_dot_w_d)
y = 8760[h] - (V_st_C_i0/V_dot_w_d)
 
IF (hour >= x) AND (hour>=y) AND (m_dot_ST_discharge_max > m_dot_w_d) THEN
 
FCmode$ = 'State 4' 
m_dot_a = 0 [kg/s]
m_dot_w = m_dot_w_d
m_dot_ST_charge = 0 [kg/s] 
m_dot_ST_discharge = m_dot_w_d

m_dot_w_FC = m_dot_w_FC

"#####################################################################"
subprogram Limit(m_dot_fan_nom1,T1, T3, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a,UA_0, UA_100 : T11 )
"! Limit
Calculate at which ambient temperature the FC at max air flow can supply demand (mass flow water = m_dot_w_d)"
"Assumptions"
m_dot_a = m_dot_fan_nom1
T3FC = T3
Q_dot_d = Q_dot_FC
 
"Calculations"
cap_speed = ((UA - UA_0)/(UA_100 - UA_0))^(1/0.8)
cap_speed = m_dot_a / m_dot_fan_nom1 
 
h1=enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T1)
h3FC=enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T3FC)
h11=enthalpy(air_HA,p=p_a,T=T11)
h12=enthalpy(air_HA,p=p_a,T=T12)
 
Q_dot_FC = UA*LMTD
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_w*(h1-h3FC)
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_a*(h12-h11)
 
DELTAT1 = T1-T12
DELTAT2 = T3FC-T11
DELTAT_pinch = min(DELTAT1, DELTAT2)
"pinch temperature"
LMTD = ( (DELTAT1^0.3275 + DELTAT2^0.3275) / 2 )^(1/0.3275)
 
end
"#####################################################################"
 
subprogram FCmaxAirST(m_dot_fan_nom1, T1, T3, T11, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100 : Q_dot_FC, 
m_dot_a,m_dot_w, UA,cap_speed, T3FC, T12 )
"! State 1a
Calculate the maximum FC for storage"
"Assumptions"
T3FC = T3
m_dot_a = m_dot_fan_nom1
 
"Calculations"
cap_speed = ((UA - UA_0)/(UA_100 - UA_0))^(1/0.8)
cap_speed = m_dot_a / m_dot_fan_nom1 
 
h1=enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T1)
h3FC=enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T3FC)
h11=enthalpy(air_HA,p=p_a,T=T11)
h12=enthalpy(air_HA,p=p_a,T=T12)
 
Q_dot_FC = UA*LMTD
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_w*(h1-h3FC)
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_a*(h12-h11)
 
DELTAT1 = T1-T12
DELTAT2 = T3FC-T11
DELTAT_pinch = min(DELTAT1, DELTAT2)
"pinch temperature"
LMTD = ( (DELTAT1^0.3275 + DELTAT2^0.3275) / 2 )^(1/0.3275)
 
$UpdateGuesses
end
"#####################################################################"
subprogram FCvarAirST(m_dot_fan_nom1, T1, T3, T11, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100,
m_dot_ST_charge_max : Q_dot_FC, m_dot_a,m_dot_w, UA,cap_speed, T3FC, T12 )
"! State 1b
Calculate the throttled FC for storage"
"Assumptions"
T3FC = T3
180
APPENDIX J. EES MODEL - SYSTEM 3

m_dot_w = m_dot_w_d + m_dot_ST_charge_max
 
"Calculations"
cap_speed = ((UA - UA_0)/(UA_100 - UA_0))^(1/0.8)
cap_speed = m_dot_a / m_dot_fan_nom1 
 
h1=enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T1)
h3FC=enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T3FC)

h12=enthalpy(air_HA,p=p_a,T=T12)

"#####################################################################"
 
subprogram FCmaxAirT3(T1, T3, T11, m_dot_w_d, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, UA_0, UA_100, m_dot_fan_nom1 : Q_dot_FC, 
m_dot_a,m_dot_w, UA,cap_speed, T3FC, T12 )
"! State 3
Calculate the maximum mass flow rate water, which the FC can cool from T1->T3"
"Assumptions"
T3FC = T3
m_dot_a = m_dot_fan_nom1
 
"Calculations"
cap_speed = ((UA - UA_0)/(UA_100 - UA_0))^(1/0.8)
cap_speed = m_dot_a / m_dot_fan_nom1 
 
h1=enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T1)
h3FC=enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T3FC)
h11=enthalpy(air_HA,p=p_a,T=T11)
h12=enthalpy(air_HA,p=p_a,T=T12)
 
Q_dot_FC = UA*LMTD
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_w*(h1-h3FC)
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_a*(h12-h11)
 
DELTAT1 = T1-T12
DELTAT2 = T3FC-T11
DELTAT_pinch = min(DELTAT1, DELTAT2)
"pinch temperature"
LMTD = ( (DELTAT1^0.3275 + DELTAT2^0.3275) / 2 )^(1/0.3275)
 
$UpdateGuesses
end
 
"#####################################################################"
 
SUBPROGRAM MIXTEMP( UA_100, UA_0, T1, T3, T11, Q_dot_d, p_w, p_a, DELTAT_pinch_C, DELTAT_pinch_E, 
DELTAT_EtoCmin, DELTAT_offset, eta_ct,W_dot_fan_nom1, m_dot_fan_nom1 : Q_dot_FC,Q_dot_VCC, m_dot_a,
m_dot_w_FC,m_dot_w_VCC, UA,cap_speed, T3FC,T3VCC, T12, T_E, T_C )
 
"assumption"
m_dot_a = m_dot_fan_nom1
T3VCC = T3 - DELTAT_offset
T3FC = T3
 
"! CALCULATION "
T_E = T3VCC - DELTAT_pinch_E 
 
181
==PAGE:196==
File:C:\Users\Rasmus\Desktop\System3.EES
6/24/2016 4:36:34 AM  Page 7
EES Ver. 10.055: #0780: Department of Energy Engineering, Tech. Univ. of Denmark
h1 = enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T1)
h3 = enthalpy(water,p=p_w,T=T3)
h3FC = enthalpy(water, p=p_w,T=T3FC)
h3VCC = enthalpy(water, p=p_w,T=T3VCC)
h11 = enthalpy(air_ha,p=p_a,T=T11)
h12 = enthalpy(air_ha,p=p_a,T=T12)
 
m_dot_w_d = Q_dot_d / (h1-h3) 
 
cap_speed = ((UA - UA_0)/(UA_100 - UA_0))^(1/0.8)
cap_speed = m_dot_a / m_dot_fan_nom1 
 
DELTAT1 = T1 - T12
DELTAT2 = T3FC - T11
LMTD = ( (DELTAT1^0.3275 + DELTAT2^0.3275) / 2 )^(1/0.3275)
 
Q_dot_FC = UA * LMTD
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_a * (h12 - h11)
Q_dot_FC = m_dot_w_FC * (h1 - h3FC)
 
m_dot_w_d = m_dot_w_FC + m_dot_w_VCC
//m_dot_w_d*h3 = m_dot_w_FC*h3FC + m_dot_w_VCC*h3VCC
 
Q_dot_d = Q_dot_FC + Q_dot_VCC
 
T_C = max( T_E+DELTAT_EtoCmin,  T11+DELTAT_pinch_C)
 
END
"#####################################################################"
